***jukebox.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jukebox.html>jukebox</a> (17020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1939, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">juke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roadside <a href = vnd.unilang:café.html>café</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:box.html>box</a></i>, replacing <a href = vnd.unilang:older.html>older</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nickel-in-a-slot <a href = vnd.unilang:phonograph.html>phonograph</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***jullie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a> (72)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">jelui</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>you</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lui.html>lui</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:people.html>people</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a></strong> (<i>unstressed <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></b>, <i>reflexive <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></b>, <i>possessive <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a></strong></b>, <i>unstressed possessive <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></b>)

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jungle.html>jungle</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi"><a href = vnd.unilang:hindi.html>Hindi</a></a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">जंगल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jaṅgal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urdu" class="extiw" title="w:Urdu"><a href = vnd.unilang:urdu.html>Urdu</a></a></span> <i class="ur-Arab mention" lang="ur">جنگل</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ur-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jangal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">जङ्गल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jaṅgala</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arid, <a href = vnd.unilang:sterile.html>sterile</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:desert.html>desert</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jurk.html>jurk</a> (1242)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaak.html>kaak</a> (7770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kekǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kēkǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kakǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaukǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*keukǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaw.html>jaw</a>; palate; pharynx</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵyewh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chew.html>chew</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Sooke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheek.html>cheek</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tsjeak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaw.html>jaw</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheek.html>cheek</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">käke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaw.html>jaw</a>; jowl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">kjake</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaw.html>jaw</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kók</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mouth.html>mouth</a>;
